Updated: September 24, 2022

Its value is what you can trade for whether they are of equal or similar value. You can trade multiple smaller valued items for bigger valued items or vice versa. "1" could be traded for a GBC (Gift Box Mystery Capsule) which give boxes which is what is needed, most of the time, to trade. 2ː1 could be any ratio (3:1, 4:1 up to 7:1) which is, at minimum, 2 similarly valued items for something valued at 1 or for 1 GBC or 125-200 NC custom. 1 GBC = 200 (125 minimum) NC custom, 2 GBCs = 400, etc.

Gift boxes can also be obtained through NC card redemptions or randomly through playing Trudy's Surprise but Trudy is a main account only activity. Gift boxes themselves are No Trade so you cannot trade a gift box with a gift box. If you want to get rid of boxes, keep sending and accepting to yourself. NC gifts have no expiration. Gifts rejected have the gift and gift box returned to the sender.

You can only trade NC items for NC items or a custom (a user spends their Neocash for desired items currently in the NC Mall) or vice versa. You cannot trade NC items for Neopoints (items) or vice versa. If a custom is involved, the non-custom trader sends their end of the trade first then the custom spender buys and sends their end. Once both parties have sent their item(s), either is fine to accept first; one doesn't accept first then send their end unless necessary and agreed upon.

Items can be obtained by purchasing from the NC Mall or multiple wearable items from unlockable token items for a NC side event. Wearable items do routinely retire but could be re-released through gambling a mystery capsule (non-GBC).

You are free to make a Value Check board at the NC Mall board.

Items not listed here could be Unwearables, No-Trade items, Popular/HTF (Hard To Find) or brand new items released after the update listed above.

You can find potential trades at either
https://items.jellyneo.net/
or
https://impress-2020.openneo.net/
DTI v JN
